const { useState } = React; const C = { teal:"#1B6B6B",tealMid:"#2A8F8F",tealLt:"#E4F4F4", sage:"#4A9B7F",sageLt:"#EAF5F0", amber:"#E8A23A",amberLt:"#FEF6E7", slate:"#3D4F5C",ink:"#1C2B33", mist:"#F4F9F8",white:"#FFFFFF",border:"#D6E8E5", red:"#C0392B",redLt:"#FDECEA", purple:"#7B6ED6",blue:"#2980B9",orange:"#E67E22", }; // ── Pediatric Growth References (WHO + CDC + Fenton) ────────────── // WHO BMI-for-age z-score reference: median (M) and approx SD by age (years) const WHO_BMI_REF={ boys:{2:[16.0,1.5],3:[15.6,1.4],4:[15.3,1.3],5:[15.3,1.3],6:[15.3,1.4],7:[15.5,1.5],8:[15.7,1.7],9:[16.0,1.9],10:[16.4,2.1],11:[16.9,2.3],12:[17.5,2.5],13:[18.2,2.7],14:[19.0,2.8],15:[19.8,2.9],16:[20.5,3.0],17:[21.1,3.0],18:[21.7,3.1],19:[22.1,3.1]}, girls:{2:[15.7,1.4],3:[15.4,1.4],4:[15.3,1.4],5:[15.2,1.4],6:[15.3,1.5],7:[15.5,1.7],8:[15.8,1.9],9:[16.3,2.1],10:[16.9,2.3],11:[17.5,2.5],12:[18.3,2.6],13:[19.0,2.7],14:[19.6,2.8],15:[20.2,2.8],16:[20.6,2.9],17:[20.9,2.9],18:[21.0,3.0],19:[21.1,3.0]}, }; function pedGrowthStatus(bmi,age,gender){ const a=Math.round(parseFloat(age)); const g=(gender==="Female")?"girls":"boys"; const ref=WHO_BMI_REF[g]; if(!ref[a]||!bmi) return null; const [M,SD]=ref[a]; const z=((parseFloat(bmi)-M)/SD); let label,color,std; // WHO 5-19 cutoffs (BMI-for-age z) if(a>=5){ if(z<-3){label="Severe thinness";color="#C0392B";} else if(z<-2){label="Thinness";color="#E67E22";} else if(z<=1){label="Normal";color="#4A9B7F";} else if(z<=2){label="Overweight";color="#E8A23A";} else{label="Obese";color="#C0392B";} std="WHO 5–19y"; }else{ // WHO 0-5 weight-for-height style cutoffs (approx via BMI-for-age) if(z<-3){label="Severely wasted";color="#C0392B";} else if(z<-2){label="Wasted";color="#E67E22";} else if(z<=2){label="Normal";color="#4A9B7F";} else if(z<=3){label="Risk of overweight";color="#E8A23A";} else{label="Overweight/Obese";color="#C0392B";} std=(a<2)?"WHO 0–2y":"WHO 2–5y"; } return {z:z.toFixed(2),label,color,std,M:M.toFixed(1)}; } const async function supaInsert(record){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/patients",{ method:"POST", headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json","apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY,"Prefer":"return=representation"}, body:JSON.stringify(record) }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Save failed: "+await res.text());} return await res.json(); } async function supaList(){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/patients?select=*&order=created_at.desc",{ headers:{"apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY} }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Load failed: "+await res.text());} return await res.json(); } async function supaDelete(id){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/patients?id=eq."+id,{ method:"DELETE", headers:{"apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY} }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Delete failed: "+await res.text());} return true; } // ── Reference Library (Supabase) ────────────────────────────────── async function refInsert(record){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/nutrition_references",{ method:"POST", headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json","apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY,"Prefer":"return=representation"}, body:JSON.stringify(record) }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Save ref failed: "+await res.text());} return await res.json(); } async function refList(){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/nutrition_references?select=*&order=created_at.desc",{ headers:{"apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY} }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Load refs failed: "+await res.text());} return await res.json(); } async function refUpdate(id,patch){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/nutrition_references?id=eq."+id,{ method:"PATCH", headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json","apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY}, body:JSON.stringify(patch) }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Update ref failed: "+await res.text());} return true; } async function refDelete(id){ const res=await fetch(SUPA_URL+"/rest/v1/nutrition_references?id=eq."+id,{ method:"DELETE", headers:{"apikey":SUPA_KEY,"Authorization":"Bearer "+SUPA_KEY} }); if(!res.ok){throw new Error("Delete ref failed: "+await res.text());} return true; } // Use the AI to extract text from an uploaded PDF (base64) — one-time at upload async function extractPdfText(base64,apiKey){ const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{ method:"POST", headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json","x-api-key":apiKey,"anthropic-version":"2023-06-01","anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access":"true"}, body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-6",max_tokens:8000,messages:[{role:"user",content:[ {type:"document",source:{type:"base64",media_type:"application/pdf",data:base64}}, {type:"text",text:"Extract the key clinical/nutritional guidance from this document as concise plain text (guidelines, targets, food lists, protocols). const MORBIDITIES = [ "Type 2 Diabetes","Hypertension","Dyslipidaemia","Hypothyroidism", "PCOS","NAFLD","CKD","Gout","IBS","Anaemia","Osteoporosis","Heart Disease","Sleep Apnea", ]; function bmi(w,h){const hm=parseFloat(h)/100,wk=parseFloat(w);return(!hm||!wk)?"":(wk/(hm*hm)).toFixed(1);} function bmiLabel(b){ const n=parseFloat(b); Check API key and billing credit at console.anthropic.com");} let cleaned=text.replace(/```json|```/g,"").trim(); let parsed=null; // Attempt 1: parse as-is try{ parsed=JSON.parse(cleaned); }catch(e1){ parsed=null; } // Attempt 2: bracket-balance repair if(!parsed){ try{ let r=cleaned; const lb=r.lastIndexOf("}"); if(lb>0) r=r.slice(0,lb+1); const oc=(r.match(/{/g)||[]).length, cc=(r.match(/}/g)||[]).length; const os=(r.match(/\[/g)||[]).length, cs=(r.match(/]/g)||[]).length; for(let i=0;i<(os-cs);i++)r+="]"; for(let i=0;i<(oc-cc);i++)r+="}"; parsed=JSON.parse(r); }catch(e2){ parsed=null; } } // Attempt 3: salvage complete days only — rebuild minimal valid JSON if(!parsed){ try{ // grab everything up to the days array const daysIdx=cleaned.indexOf('"days"'); // extract each complete day object {"day":...total":N} const dayRe=/\{\s*"day"[\s\S]*?"total"\s*:\s*\d+\s*\}/g; const dayMatches=cleaned.match(dayRe)||[]; // extract summary if present let summaryObj={}; const sumMatch=cleaned.match(/"summary"\s*:\s*(\{[\s\S]*?\})\s*,\s*"(?:flags|days|supplements|keyPrinciples)"/); if(sumMatch){ try{ summaryObj=JSON.parse(sumMatch[1]); }catch(e){} } if(dayMatches.length>0){ const daysJson=dayMatches.join(","); const rebuilt='{"summary":'+(sumMatch?sumMatch[1]:'{}')+',"flags":[],"supplements":[],"keyPrinciples":[],"days":['+daysJson+']}'; parsed=JSON.parse(rebuilt); parsed._partial=dayMatches.length; } }catch(e3){ parsed=null; } } if(!parsed){ throw new Error("The plan response was cut off and could not be recovered. Please pick a single language (English OR Arabic, not Both) and try again."); } parsed._date=new Date().toLocaleDateString("en-GB",{day:"numeric",month:"long",year:"numeric"}); parsed._planLang=planLang; parsed._patient={name,dob,bmi:BMI,gender,caseLabel:caseObj?caseObj[lang]||caseObj.en:"",dietLabel:dietObj?dietObj[lang]||dietObj.en:""}; if(parsed._partial){setSaveMsg((ar?"⚠️ تم استرداد ":"⚠️ Recovered ")+parsed._partial+(ar?" أيام فقط — جرب لغة واحدة لخطة كاملة":" days only — pick one language for a full 7-day plan"));} setPlan(parsed);setStep(4);setSavedToDb(false); setSaveMsg(ar?"✏️ راجعي وعدّلي الخطة ثم اضغطي حفظ":"✏️ Review and edit the plan, then click Save"); }catch(e){setErr("Error: "+e.message);} finally{setLoading(false);} } async function loadHistory(){ setLoadingSaved(true);setShowHistory(true); try{ const list=await supaList(); setSavedPatients(list); }catch(e){setErr("Could not load history: "+e.message);} finally{setLoadingSaved(false);} } function openSavedPatient(p){ const pl=p.plan; pl._date=pl._date||new
